Ao conectar-se a um servidor VPN por meio do Hotspot Shield VPN Proxy, por exemplo, é estabelecida uma conexão protegida e criptografada a um servidor em outro país. Devido ao processo de criptografia, os dados não podem ser filtrados ou bloqueados.\r\n\r\n* Por que usar uma VPN\r\nCom uma VPN, você não apenas é capaz de desbloquear serviços censurados ou restritos geograficamente como Facebook, Pandora e Youtube, mas também mantém sua privacidade e segurança online totalmente amparadas, navegando na rede de forma completamente anônima.\r\n\r\n* VPN versus Proxy\r\nAmbos VPN e Proxy podem ocultar a identidade do usuário através do redirecionamento do tráfego da internet e da mudança de IP. Contudo, um servidor proxy é totalmente baseado no navegador e pode não ser compatível com certas páginas da web com tecnologia não baseada em navegadores. Diferentemente de um proxy, o serviço VPN criptografa todo o seu tráfego e trabalha com todos os serviços baseados na internet. is a brand-new title from the creators of This War of Mine. It’s a society survival game that asks what people are capable of when pushed to the brink of extinction. In an entirely frozen world, people develop steam-powered technology to oppose the overwhelming cold. The city’s ruler has to manage both the citizens and the infrastructure they live in. The leader’s tactical skills face challenges that will frequently question morality and the basic foundations of what we consider organized society. Optimization and resource management often clash with empathy and thoughtful decision-making. While city and society management will consume most of the ruler’s time, at some point exploration of the outside world is necessary to understand its history and present state.\r\n\r\nWhat decisions will you make to ensure the survival of your society? What will you do when pushed to the limit? And...\r\n\r\n...who will you become in the process?\r\n\r\nMAKE THE LAW\r\nSociety is a group of people who abide by the same rules and share similar beliefs. Establish laws that regulate the existence of your growing society. Decide on their working routine, healthcare, food provision and other crucial aspects of everyday life. Maintain their hope and contentment – the moral condition of your society is as important as securing the basic means to keep them fed and safe.\r\n\r\nWEIGH UP YOUR CHOICES\r\nSome of your decisions will seem small – like deciding the fate of a troubled citizen or meeting the demands of a newborn faction – but be aware that the sum of your doings can lead to unexpected results. Your people put their faith in you, but their devotion is not limitless. Leadership can be a burden.\r\n\r\nDEVELOP NEW TECHNOLOGIES\r\nSurvival demands progress. React to current events, but don’t forget about the long term and investing in development and technological progress. Providing a highly advanced infrastructure with self-powered automatons, airships and other technical wonders is difficult, but achievable. It all depends on your management and leadership skills.\r\n\r\nEXPLORE THE FROSTLAND\r\nWhile New London is your main focus, there is much more to the world than what lies within the limits of your city. Expeditions, while risky, can bring you valuable intel, precious supplies and grow your society’s population. There may be people out there, and their fate lies solely in your hands.\r\n\r\nSHAPE YOUR SOCIETY\r\nIf you reach a turning point, do not hesitate to determine the path of your people.
